Cc:"Fay, Chuck"<CFay@felix.filenet.com>,"Whelan, Dan"<DWhelan@felix.filenet.com>,"Green, Jim"<JGreen@felix.filenet.com>,"Palmer, Ann"<APalmer@felix.filenet.com>,"Johnson, Andrew"<AJohnson@felix.filenet.com>,"Tucker, Michael"<MTucker@felix.filenet.com>,"Fink, Evangeline"<EFink@felix.filenet.com>

The next V&V meeting will be hosted by FileNET in
Costa Mesa California, on October 1 and 2 from
9 am to 5 pm Pacific time.

If you plan to attend, please e-mail me ASAP so I
can order the catered lunches.
There is a sandwich place called the Business Park Cafe 
only a couple of minutes walk away. So you will have 
the option of going there for lunch instead of eating 
the catered lunch (unless we decide to work through 
lunch).

The following file has directions from three airports, 
hotel information, and local maps. The closest airport
is John Wayne Orange County airport. Use that airport
if you can get a flight. The second closest (and
second choice) is Long Beach airport. Since the following
file has no directions from Long Beach airport,
get in touch with me if you want to use the Long
Beach airport. LAX and Ontario airport are a ways away.

 <<Directions.doc>> 
The meeting will be held in "FileNET building 4" of the
Harbor Gateway business complex on the second floor 
in room 2349:

 <<Bldg4.doc>> 
Enter the lobby, and take the door on the left.
Both doors have a badge reader. I will prop the left
door open until 9 am on Monday and Tuesday. If you're
late, use the phone in the lobby, dial 5883, and ask 
our sectary Nelsy to please come down and let you in
to the WEBDAV Versioning and Variants meeting.
There is no receptionist in building 4. We're not going
to issue badges.

Enter the door on the left, turn left, go up the stairs,
go about half way down the corridor, and it's on
your right. It's a large room.

The room has power for laptops, whiteboards,
an overhead projector, and an LCD screen to project
what's on your laptop screen using the overhead projector.
So, it will be possible to presentations without
printing them out. We can also have the secretaries
print things out and make copies.

I am assuming Jim Whitehead will supply the agenda.

If you have any questions, get in touch with me.

Alan Babich
ABabich@filenet.com
714-966-3403
